      <section class="block block-views clearfix" id="block-views-homepage-carousel-block">
       <div class="view view-homepage-carousel view-id-homepage_carousel view-display-id-block view-dom-id-bda62f3d5cfb22ce8f6f260471ac9598">
        <div class="view-content">
         <div class="views-row views-row-1 views-row-odd views-row-first views-row-last">
          <div class="carousel slide" id="carousel-bootstrap">
           <div class="bullets-control">
            <ol class="carousel-indicators">
             <li class="bullet active" data-slide-to="0" data-target="#carousel-bootstrap">
             </li>
             <li class="bullet " data-slide-to="1" data-target="#carousel-bootstrap">
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="carousel-inner">
            <div class="item active">
             <img alt="American Antiquarian Society Historical Periodicals Collection logo." src="https://mndigital.org/sites/mndigital.org/files/carousel_images/AAS.png"/>
             <div class="carousel-caption">
              <h2>
               New Research Resource
              </h2>
              <p>
               Minitex now has access to the Historical Periodicals Collection from The American Antiquarian Society. This selection of over 6,500 primary source titles from the years 1684-1912 provides a fascinating window into the history of our country. The collection is available through Minitex's
               <a href="http://www.elm4you.org/">
                Electronic Library for Minnesota (ELM) portal
               </a>
               .
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="item">
             <img alt="Primary Source Sets image." src="https://mndigital.org/sites/mndigital.org/files/carousel_images/primary-source-sets.jpg"/>
             <div class="carousel-caption">
              <h2>
               Primary Source Sets Now Available!
              </h2>
              <p>
               <a href="/projects/primary-source-sets">
                Primary Source Sets
               </a>
               are curated collections of primary sources from Minnesota Reflections. Modeled after the
               <a href="http://dp.la/primary-source-sets">
                Digital Public Library of America's similar project
               </a>
               , they are designed to help students develop critical thinking skills by exploring a variety of topics related to Minnesota history and culture.
               <a href="/projects/primary-source-sets">
                Browse the initial collection
               </a>
               and check out the
               <a href="https://news.minitex.umn.edu/news/reference-outreach-instruction/new-minnesota-reflections-primary-source-sets-now-available">
                Minitex News article
               </a>
               to learn more about our new project.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <!-- .carousel-inner -->
           <!--  next and previous controls here
           href values must reference the id for this carousel -->
           <a class="carousel-control left" data-slide="prev" href="#carousel-bootstrap">
            <i class="fa fa-caret-left fa-3x">
            </i>
           </a>
           <a class="carousel-control right" data-slide="next" href="#carousel-bootstrap">
            <i class="fa fa-caret-right fa-3x">
            </i>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>
